## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# TypeScript Module Resolution Migration from Classic to Node16

## Your Task

Find all TypeScript source files in microsoft/TypeScript under src/compiler/ that implement module resolution. Identify: the moduleNameResolver entry point and its strategy dispatch (Classic vs Node vs Node16 vs Bundler), the node16ModuleNameResolver and its package.json exports field resolution, the classicNameResolver, the getPackageJsonInfo helper, the pathPatternMatch for path mapping, and the tracing/diagnostic reporting for resolution failures. Report each file path and key function or class.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/TypeScript--v5.7.2.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

Perfect! I've created a comprehensive analysis of the TypeScript module resolution system in `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Findings

**Primary File**: `src/compiler/moduleNameResolver.ts` contains all the core module resolution logic.

**Entry Point & Strategy Dispatch**: 
- `resolveModuleName()` is the main function that dispatches to different resolution strategies based on ModuleResolutionKind (Node16, NodeNext, Node10, Classic, Bundler)

**Node16/NodeNext Resolution**:
- `node16ModuleNameResolver` and `nodeNextModuleNameResolver` delegate to `nodeNextModuleNameResolverWorker` and then `nodeModuleNameResolverWorker`
- Supports conditional exports, imports, pattern trailers, and ESM mode detection

**Package.json Exports Field**:
- `loadModuleFromExports()` handles main entry point exports
- `loadModuleFromExportsOrImports()` implements pattern matching
- `comparePatternKeys()` sorts patterns per Node.js spec
- Supports conditional exports with target resolution

**Classic Resolution**:
- `classicNameResolver()` provides legacy TypeScript behavior with ancestor directory walking

**Path Mapping**:
- `tryLoadModuleUsingPaths()` matches against path patterns
- Uses `matchPatternOrExact` from utilities.ts for pattern matching

**Package.json Handling**:
- `getPackageJsonInfo()` with lazy-loaded fields
- `getPackageScopeForPath()` finds containing package.json
- Caching system in ModuleResolutionCache

**Tracing & Diagnostics**:
- `trace()` and `isTraceEnabled()` manage resolution tracing
- `ModuleResolutionState` carries diagnostic reporting

I've documented 47 symbols and created a complete chain showing the resolution flow from entry point through to package.json exports field resolution.
